236 _Bhajanamritam 1_

```
Sri Krishna is a Name dear to Thee. Natavaralala (one who loves
to dance) is a Name dear to Thee. Munijanapala (Protector of
the sages) is a Name dear to Thee.
```

**Éri rÀMA nÀMAMu**

**érì ràma nàmamu**

**entòmañchi madhuramu**

**madhuràdi madhuramu**

**manakaåde amätamu (érì ràma)**

```
Sri Rama’s name is very sweet. It is so sweet like ambrosia,
also easily reachable.
```

**tàâaki mardinchi munulanu**

**kàpàdina nàmamu**

**äàttini nàtika màrchina**

**ramya maina nàmamu (érì ràma)**

```
Rama killed evil demoness Tataki. He made into a stone a
woman. That is the beauty of this name.
```

**äàvanàdi ràkçasùlanu**

**vadhiyimchina nàmamu**

**vàsiga bhadràchalamuna (érì ràma)**

```
He killed Ravana and other rakshakas and he is happily staying
in Bhadrachala.
```

**Éri rÀMA rÀMA nÀMAM**

**“érì ràma ràmà nàmam janma rakçaka mantram**

**japippavarkk ànandam paramànandam”**

**bhajikkuka manamè nì! ninakku sadgati nèâàn**

**orikkalum maäakkàte bhajikkuka nì.. .. (érì ràma)**

```
Devotional songs 237
```

```
O mind, always chant Rama Mantram which will take one to
the Goal of life and which will give Supreme Bliss to one who
ever chants It.
```

**eååamatta janmam etra maååitil vätha kalaññu?**

**khinnathaykkorantyaminnum vannatillaho!**

**janmaminnu dhanyamàkum puåya nàma**

**mantramòti nirmalatvamayi manassè chinta**

**cheyyukil (érì ràma)**

```
Innumerable lives have been spent on this earth but sorrow has
not come to an end. By chanting this holy mantra, one becomes
pure and the purpose of life will be fulfilled.
```

**érì raghupati nàmam ràghava (jànaki) érì ràmam**

**srita janàérayaràmam bhaja manamè!**

**danuja ripu nàmam, vimala hädayaràmam,**

**durita haraåa nàmam bhajamanamè! (érì ràma)**

```
O mind, worship that Rama who is Raghava and who is the
Refuge of those who take refuge in Him. Worship that Rama
who is the enemy of demons, who is pure in heart and whose
Name removes all miseries.
```

**Éri rÀMAcHAnDrA**

**érì ràmachandra - raghu ràmachandra**

**prabhu ràmachandra bhagavàn...!**

**érì dhanya dhanya sìtàbhiràma**

**sukritàtma rùpa ràma...! (érì ràma)**

```
O Sri Ramachandra, Thou of Raghu’s dynasty, Lord Ramachandra,
O God, the blessed and auspicious Beloved of Sita, whose Form
is the very soul of the pious...
```

238 _Bhajanamritam 1_

**hè... jànakì ramaåa ràghavà**

**vimala vìra sùryakula jàtà...**

**hè... ràma ràma raghuvìra ràma**

**karuåardra nètra ràmà...!**

**érì ràma ràma jaya ràma ràma**

**jaya ràma ràma jaya ràma... (érì ràma)**

```
O Delighter of Sita (Janaki), taintless One who was born in the
dynasty of the Sun and glorified for His strength and bravery, O
Rama, with eyes moistened by compassion... Lord Rama, Rama,
Rama, victory to Rama, Rama, victory to Rama...
```

**hè... mauktikà bharaåa bhùshita -bhuvana**

**saundaryàtma ràma**

**ànandarùpa - nigamàntasàra**

**nikhilàtmarùpa ràma**

**érì ràma ràma jaya ràma ràma**

**jaya ràma ràma jaya ràma... (érì ràma)**

```
O Rama who wears ornaments of pearl, who is the Jewel of the
world, Bliss Incarnate, the Quintessence of the Upanishads, the
integral form of all souls...
```

```
Lord Rama, Rama, Rama, victory to Rama, Rama, victory to
Rama...
```

**Éri VinÀYAKA**

**érì vinàyaka guha jananì.. .. .. amba**

**érìmkàràrcchita pañchadaéàkçari**

```
O Mother of Ganesha and Subrahmanium, Who art worshipped
by the 15 syllable mantra...
```

**hrìm kàriåi himagiri nandinì**

```
Devotional songs 239
```

**hìràñchita vibhùçaåàngì**

**màhèévarì mahiçavinàéinì........**

**màm pàlaya pàlaya varadè........**

```
O Thou art worshipped with the sound ‘Hrim’, who art the
daughter of the Himalaya Mountain, whose limbs are decorated
with diamonds, O Great Goddess, Destroyer of the demon
Mahisha, O Giver of boons, please protect me, protect me!
```

**mòdànvitè dama éama dàyinì**

**nàdàêkurè naîina nivàéini**

**nìtàn mama éòkavinàéini**

**pàdàmbujè layamaruîuka tàyè**

```
O Blissful One who bestows control of mind and senses, who
art born of Sound, who dwells in the lotus, only Thou art the
destroyer of my sorrows. O Mother. Please bless me to merge
in Thy Lotus Feet.
```

**sÄÇtiYuM nÌYe**

**säçtiyum nìyè säçtàvum nìyè**

**éaktiyum nìyè satyavum (or nityavym) nìye**

**dèvì...dèvì...dèvì**

```
Creation and Creator art Thou, Thou art Energy and Truth... O
Goddess, O Goddess, O Goddess!
```

**aåáa kaâàha vidhàtàvum nìyè**

**àdiyu mantavum, nìyè (säçtiyum)**

```
Creatress of the Cosmos art Thou, and Thou art the beginning
and end.
```

**paramàåu chaitanyapporùîùm nìyè**

**pañcha bhùtangaîum nìyè (säçtiyum)**

```
The Essence of the individual soul art Thou, and Thou art the
five elements as well.
```

240 _Bhajanamritam 1_

**sunDArÌ nÌ VÀYÒ**

**sundarì nì vàyò......**

**purandarì nì vàyo......**

**éaêkarì nì vàyo......**

**nirantarì nì vàyo......**

```
Please come, O Beautiful One. Consort of Shiva, please come.
O Auspicious One, please come. Please come, O Endless One.
```

**skandan tantaykku vàmàkçi nì ennum**

**kànti pùratte chintum kàmàkçi nì**

**bandhuvàyi kàåmòrkku svantam nìyè - en**

**chintaykku muäavàyì ninnìâammà...... (sundarì)**

```
O Vamakshi, Consort of Lord Shiva, O Kamakshi who radiates
brilliance everywhere, to those who look upon Thee as their dear
Relation, Thou art their very own. O Mother, please remain as
the spring of my inspiration.
```

**onnàyi palatàyi arùpavu màyi**

**ninnàlum jyòtirmayì brahmam nìyè......**

**nannàyen uîîam nì aäiyillayò**

**chonnàlum munnil nì varukillayò? (sundarì)**

```
Being both of one and of many forms, Thou art the Light of the
Absolute. Knowest Thou not my heart well? Won’t Thou come
before me even though I ask?
```

**sVÀGAtAM KÄÇÅA**

**svàgatam käçåà éaranàgatam käçåà**

**madhuràpuri sadana mädu vadanà madhusùdanà**

**(svàgatam)**

```
Devotional songs 241
```

**bhòga dàpta sulabha supuçpa gandha kaîabhà**

**kastùri tilaka mahibhà**

**mama kandà nanda gòpa kandà... (svàgatam)**

**musâìkàsura chàåùra malla**

**malla viéàrada kuvalayà pìáha**

**narttana kàîiya mardana gòkula rakçaåa**

**sakala sulakçana dèvà**

**siçâa janapàla saêkalppa kalppa**

**kalppa éata kòâi asama baràbhava**

**dhìrà munì jana vihàrà käçåa**

**dhìrà munì jana vihàrà**

**madana sukumàrà daitya samhàra dèvà**

**madhura madhura rati sàhasa sàhasa...**

**vraja yuvatì jana mànasa pùjita**

**sa.. da.. pa.. ga.. ri.. pa.. gari.. sadhasa**

**tiddhittikajanu taddittakajanu ta ttakayanu**

**tarikiâagugu tanakiâa taka dhim (3) (svàgatam)**

**tAVA sAnniDHÀnAttil**

**tava sannidhànattil manatàrarppicchu**

**tapassucheyyunnu ñàn aniéamammè...**

**anaévara rùpiåì...! samastalòkèévarì...!**

**anugrahikkuka enne nì... ammè**

**anugrahikkuka enne nì...! (tava)**

```
Day and night I am doing penance, my mind surrendered at Thy
Feet. O Goddess Eternal, Goddess of all the worlds, bless me,
O Mother, bless me.
```

242 _Bhajanamritam 1_

**surajana paripùjita nì... dìna jana-**

**mànasattinu taå alum nì...**

**tiru nàmabhajanam cheytuåarum éuddha-**

**hädayattil niäajñànam nì...**

**mama jananì... jaya jananì...**

**jaya jaya jananì... jaya jaya jananì (tava)**

```
Thou art the One worshipped by the gods as well as the Shelter
for distressed hearts. In the hearts awakened and purified by the
singing of Thy praises, Thou rise as the Knowledge Supreme.
Victory to Mother...Victory to my Mother, Victory to the Mother
of the Universe!
```

**nigamàgamam pàâum poruî nì... nityam**

**munijanamtèâum nidhi nì...**

**praåavàvarttanattinte laya nilayam nì**

**manavachassoâuêgunnòriâavum nì...**

**mama jananì... jaya jananì...**

**jaya jaya jananì... jaya jaya jananì (tava)**

```
Thou art the Truth that the Vedas and Sastras sing of and the
Treasure ever sought by ascetics. It is in Thee that the vibration
of OM dissolves, speech and mind lose themselves in Thee. Oh
my Mother...Victory to Mother, Victory to Mother...Victory to
the Mother of the Universe!
```

**tÀYÈ tAVA tAnAYAril**

**tàyè tava tanayaril**

**kàruåyamèlàykayàl**

**tàpam hädi vaîarunnu**

**kàruåyarùpànganè**

```
O ever youthful Mother, because Thou are not showering mercy
on Thy children, grief is intensifying in their hearts.
```

```
Devotional songs 243
```

**mègham kèäi divàkara prabhaye**

**mùâum kaåakkenna pòl**

**mòhattil vìåàzhàn**

**viâallè kàruåya rùpàêganè**

```
O ever youthful Mother, allow me not to fail and sink down due
to delusion like the sun that gets covered by clouds.
```

**tàrum nìrum taruvum**

**akhila jìvajàlaêgaîum**

**nin màyayennaäiyunnu**

**ñàn kàruåya rùpàêganè**

```
O ever youthful One, I know that flowers, water, trees and all
living beings are Thy Maya.
```

**ulAKAttinÀDHÀrA**

**ulakattinàdhàrapporuî nìyamma**

**guåa miyalunna nayanattinoîi nìyamma**

```
O Mother, Thou art the Essence of the Substratum of the world.
O Mother, Thou art the Light of virtuous eyes.
```

**takarunna hädayattin abhayam amma**

**aäivinnum uäavàyoraäivum amma - ellàm aäi...**

```
For breaking hearts Thou art the Refuge, O Mother. The Wisdom
that is the Source of all knowledge art Thou, O Mother.
```

**aruîìâuvatinuîîa takhilum nìyè**

**akhilarkkum abhayam nin padatàr amma**

```
Give me all that is needed for that (Wisdom). Thy Feet are the
Refuge for all.
```

**kanivinnu kanivàya karuåànidhè**

**tellukäpayenni laruîìâu käpàyambudhè**

```
O Source of all mercy and Treasure of compassion, grant a bit
of Thy compassion to me.
```

244 _Bhajanamritam 1_

**uttAMA PrÈMAttin**

**uttama prèmattin paryàyamàyiâum**

**éàévatasnèha pradànamuttè**

**pàvana vàtsalyam èkunna pàvanì**

**pàdattil kaååìràl archi chìâàm**

```
Thou art the Embodiment of the Highest Love, O Giver of
Eternal Love. O Pure One who gives pure affection, I worship
Thy Feet with my tears.
```

**bhàvana kappuäamengò vilasunna**

**satya svarùpattin tèn mozhikaî**

**karååa manòharamà vachanangaîàî**

**kàtum hädayavum éàntamàyi**

```
Hearing the nectarean, joy giving words of the Embodiment of
Truth who abides beyond where thought can reach, my heart,
eyes and ears have become tranquil and quiet.
```

**à käpa varååippàn àvatil àrkkumè**

**à snèham vàkkal paäavatalla**

**à prèmam engane ñàn uracchìâuvàn**

**kaååìràl vìndum namicchìâunnèn**

```
That love can be described by none. It is beyond words. Then
how can I hope to speak about it? I can only bow down again
and again with tears in my eyes.
```

```
Devotional songs 245
```

**uYirÀYi oÎiYÀYi**

**uyiràyi oîiyàyi ulakattin muraâàyi**

**urapoêgum umayè nì eviâè...?**

**kàttàyi kaâalàyi kanalàyi nilkkum**

**en kalayè nin kanivennil illè...? (uyiràyi)**

```
O Goddess Uma, where art Thou Who art said to be the life, light
and firmness of the earth? O artful One Who exists as wind, sea
and fire, have Thou no mercy on me?
```

**aäivellàm akalunnu piäavippòl tuâarunnu**

**maäivellàm uäavàkunnù**

**kuäavellàm tikayunnu tikavutta nìyenyè**

**maäayellàm maäavàkunnù (uyiràyi)**

```
All wisdom has fled to a distance and repeated births continue.
Unreality has become reality and all defects are increasing in
the absence of Thee who art the Real Knowledge concealed.
```

**rudhiràsthi màmsattàl paritàpa durgandha-**

**ppuriye samrakçikkunnù...**

**purivàâilppuäam ellàm paripàvanam àkkunnu**

**puri nàthane aäiyunnilla...! (uyiràyi)**

```
Thou art protecting this pitiful city (the body) stinking with
blood, bone and flesh. We clean the surface of the body alone
knowing not its Lord.
```

**manamàkum vànaran madamenna kaniyumàyi**

**ninavillàtuzhaäìâunnù...?**

**tan rùpam ninayàte kàlattin kanivil nàm**

**kàlannùåàyi màäunnù...! (uyiràyi)**

```
The monkey of the mind wanders ceaselessly holding in its hand
the fruit of conceit. Reflecting not on its Real Nature it becomes
food for the God of Death.
```

246 _Bhajanamritam 1_

**VAnDÈ nAnDAKuMÀrAM**

**vandè vandè nanda kumàram**

**nanda kumàram navanìta chòram**

**vandè vandè ràdhika lòlam**

**gòpì chitta vihàram, vandè**

```
I salute the Son of Nanda, Stealer of butter, Delighter of Radha,
who resides in the minds of the Gopis!
```

**vandè vandè nanda kumàram**

**érìdhara åìéam jagadà dhàram**

**bhava bhaya dùram bhakta mandàram**

**vandè vandè ràdhika lòlam**

**gòpì chitta vihàram**

```
I salute again and again the Lord who bears the Goddess Lakshmi
on His chest, who is the Substratum of the world, Dispeller of the
fear of transmigration, Flower of the devotees heart, Delighter
of Radha who resides in the minds of the Gopis!
```

**vandè vandè nanda kumàram**

**vèåu vinòdam vèda susàram**

**karuåàlòlam kàñchana chèlam**

**kamanìya gàtram kamsa samhàram**

**yamunà tìra vihàram vandè**

**yamunà tìra vihàram**

```
I salute the One Who plays the flute, Essence of the Vedas, who
delights in showing compassion, who wears golden color robes,
of beautiful Form, Slayer of Kamsa who resides on the banks
of the Yamuna River!
```

**vändàvana sañchàram vändàvana sañchàram**

**vandè vandè nanda kumàram**

**vandè vandè ràdhikalòlam**

```
Devotional songs 247
```

```
I salute that One who moves about Vrindavan, the Son of Nanda,
Delighter of Radha!
```

**muni jana pàlam mòhana rùpam**

**muraîìlòlam madana gòpàlam**

**yamunà tìra vihàram vandè**

**vändàvana sañchàram vandè**

```
Salutations to the Protector of the sages, of enchanting form,
Lover of the flute, beautiful cowherd Boy who stays on the banks
of the Yamuna and moves about Vrindavan!
```

**VAnDiKKunnÈn**

**vandikkunnèn ammè ennil näittamàâuvàn**

**vandanìyaprabhè vannaâi paåìyunnèn**

```
In order that Thou should dance within me, O Mother, O
Adorable One, I bow and surrender to Thee.
```

**jìvàtmikayàyi ninnu jìvippikkum éaktiye**

**nì veâiññu pòyàl niéchalam akhilavum (vandi)**

```
Existing as the Power of Life within the individual soul, if Thou
should leave, all would become still.
```

**parayàm éakti và... và paripùrååànandàtmikè**

**paramajyòtissè và piriyàtennil ninnum (vandi)**

```
O Universal energy, the Self of Perfect Bliss, come, come. O
Supreme Light, remain never abandoning me.
```

**jñànakkaâalè và... và nànà säçâikàraåè**

**akhilàdhàra murttè aîavillàtta sattè (vandi)**

```
Come, come, O Ocean of Knowledge, the Cause of the Diverse
Creation, Embodiment of the Substratum of the Universe,
Measureless Essence.
```

**aåuvilumaåuvè và... và akhila vyàpta vastuvè**

**àyira daîapadmattil àvàsè nì và... và (vandi)**

248 _Bhajanamritam 1_

```
O Thou Atom of atoms, Who pervades the Universe, Dweller
in the Thousand-petalled Lotus, come, come.
```

**kòâi divàkara éòbhè en taâiyil vàzhum ambikè**

**aâiyanaviâe layìkkuvàn amma tanne àérayam**

**(vandi)**

```
Whose brilliance equals millions of suns, Dweller within myself,
that Mother alone is the only hope for getting merged in Her.
```

**amäita jyòtirmayamè ànandàbdhè ninnil**

**mànasamaniéam lìnamàkàn tuåaykkaåam (vandi)**

```
O Ambrosial Light, Ocean of Bliss, may my mind merge in
Thee forever.
```

**nirmalamè nirguåamè anudinam namiykkunnu**

**dìnadayàlò ente dìnatayakattuka (vandi)**

```
O pure and qualityless Being, I bow to Thee again and again.
Compassionate to the afflicted, rid me of my distress.
```

**aäivinnaäivè sattè abhayapradamè éivè**

**aäiyàn aäivillammè kuåáalinì... éaktì (vandi)**

```
O Knowledge of knowledge, Essence, Shive (Consort of Shiva),
giver of shelter, O Mother, Kundalini Sakti, I have not even the
knowledge to know.
```

**éaêkakaîakattàn éaêkarì nìyettaåam**

**pèyàkkolla .... enne màyike nìye... gati (vandi)**

```
O Sankari, Thou must come to remove my doubts. May I not
have the fate of a madman, O Maya.
```

**VAnnÀluM AMbiKÈ**

**vannàlum ambikè tàyè manòharì**

**tannàlum tàvaka daréanatte**

**sañchita saubhagamen chittapatmattil**

**nin chàrurùpam viîaêgiâaââe (vannàlum)**

```
Devotional songs 249
```

```
Come, O Mother, Who art the Enchantress of the mind. give
me, O Ambika, Thy Vision. Let Thy Form shine in the lotus of
my heart.
```

**ennuîîil bhaktiye chemmeyuåartunna**

**dhanyàm ponnuçassenudikkum**

**nàmam japicchu samtäptayàyennu ñàn**

**ànanda bàçpa vilòlayàkum (vannàlum)**

```
When will dawn that blessed day when my heart will become
full of devotion to Thee? Satiated with the repetition of Thy
Name, when will blissful tears flow from my eyes?
```

**màmaka chittam àtmàvum viéuddhamàyi**

**mevunna nàîennu vannuchèrum**

**mànavum màmùlum lajjayum klèéavum**

**ñàn upèkçikkunna nàî varumò (vannàlum)**

```
When will that day dawn when my mind and soul will become
pure? Then vain pride, possessiveness, bashfulness and affliction
will be relinquished.
```

**bhaktiyàkum madhumottikkuâichu ñàn**

**chikkennu prèmattàl mattayàkum**

**poââicchiricchu ñàn ànanda magnayàyi**

**peââennu kaååìru vannukezhum (vannàlum)**

```
When will I drink the nectar of devotion and becoming
intoxicated, laugh and cry immersed in bliss lost in Thee?
```

**VArAÎunnA HÄDAYAttil**

**varaîunna hädayattil kuîirmazha peyyuvàn**

**varanda jìvitam vaîamàkki màttuvàn**

**vannìâukammè ponnambikè**

**vandikkunnu ñàn varumò... varumò?**

**ennarikil nì varumö?**

250 _Bhajanamritam 1_

```
O Mother, pour forth cool rain on my parched heart that my dry
life may blossom. Come, my dear Mother, come. I bow down to
Thee. Will Thou come, will Thou come near me?
```

**innu varum, amma innu varum ennum**

**àéayòâe mantricchen hädayam**

**illa, òmalè illa ñàn ninnil nin-**

**oru nàîum akannu pòkayilla**

```
“Mother will come today, yes, Mother will come today!” Thus
my heart hopefully chants like a mantra. “No, my darling, no. I
will never go away from you.”
```

**VAsuDÈVA PutrAnÈ VÀ**

**vasudèva putranè và nìla varnna nè và**

**ì hädayattine kùriruî nìnguvàn**

**nì kaniyaåamè dèvà**

**nì kaniyaåamè**

```
O Son of Vasudeva, blue-colored One, please come. Please bless
me by dispelling the darkness of this heart.
```

**amma dèvakiyè.. kàttu koîîaåamè**

**uååi käçåane manninu nalkiya**

**puåya màrnnavaîè dèvì**

**puåya marnnavaîè...**

```
O Mother Devaki, please protect me, O holy Devi who has given
birth to Baby Krishna for the sake of the world.
```

**èzhakaîkkulakil.. .. ennum àérayamè.. ..**

**ètu kuttavum nì poäuttu**

**ñangaîil prìti koîîaåamè**

**dèvà prìti koîîaåamè.. ..**

```
O Holy One, Who art always the Support for Thy supplicants
in this world, forgiving any errors, be pleased with us, Lord, be
pleased with us...
```

```
Devotional songs 251
```

**VÈDÀMbiKÈ**

**vèdàmbikè namò nàdàmbikè**

**vandè surasaêghasèvyapàdam**

```
O Mother of the Vedas, O Mother of Sounds, I bow to Thee. I
bow to Thy Feet which are adored by the Gods.
```

**kàmapradam kamalàbhapradam**

**kadanàzhikaâattuken ràgapriyè**

```
Bestowing love, bestowing the radiance of the lotus, O Lover
of music, take me across this ocean of misery
```

**vidyè éivè sarvalòkahitè**

**madahatyè jaya bhava nàéakartrì**

```
O Goddess of Wisdom, O Parvati Who does good to all the
world, Destroyer of pride and rebirth, be victorious.
```

**màyàmayam manamàràl gatam - mama**

**àlambanam tava pàdàmbujam**

```
Thou Who art full of Maya, by whom the mind exists, Thy Lotus
Feet are my support.
```

**pràåikaîkkokkeyum pràåan ammà**

**kàryattinokkeyum kàraåam ammà**

```
Mother is the Life of all creatures. Mother is the Cause of all
things.
```

**ghòra samsàra makattiâeåam**

**dìnanàm ennè nì kattiâeåam**

```
Deign to rid me of this terrible cycle of birth and death. Protect
this miserable one.
```

**muktidè muktidè hastè namò**

**éaktè namastè mahàprabhàvè**

```
Bowing to Thee with joined palms, I pray, give me Liberation.
O Powerful One, Great Radiance, I bow to Thee.
```

252 _Bhajanamritam 1_

**VeDÀntA VÈnAl**

**vèdànta vènalilùâe**

**oru nàdànta pànthanalaññàl**

**nì tàn tuåaykkum avane enna**

**gìtàrttham ippòzh eviâè? (vèdanta)**

```
Now where is the truth of the Gita that proclaims that Thou wilt
help a traveller to Brahman through the summer of Vedanta?
```

**éàntàtmanà pada pràptikkayi**

**kàntàrasàmyapathattilkkùâi**

**nìntàn tuâaêgi ennàlum**

**chìntunnù chittam vyathayàl (vèdanta)**

```
Even though I am swimming through the forest-like way with a
peaceful soul, for the attainment of Thy Feet, my mind is filled
with sorrow.
```

**entinò vèndi hädantam sadà-**

**venturukunnàrtta bandhò...**

**chinta ninakkitilillè ente**

**santàpamokkeyum màttàn (vèdanta)**

```
O Friend of the miserable, my heart is always burning for
something, I know not what. Haven’t Thou the mind to remove
all of my sorrows?
```

**ammè bhagavatì dèvì ninte**

**chinmòhana svarùpattil**

**vannulayikkàte éàntiyil-**

**ènammè aäiyunnatillè? (vèdanta)**

```
O Mother, O Bhagavati Devi, aren’t Thou knowing that without
merging in Thy mind-enchanting Being, there is no peace?
```

```
Devotional songs 253
```

**VinÀYAKA VinÀYAKA**

**vinàyaka vinàyaka**

**viévàdhàra vinàyaka**

**siddhi vinàyaka bhava bhaya nàéa**

**suramuni vandita érì gaåèça**

vinàyaka = Destroyer of obstacles.

viévàdhàra = The Substratum of the universe.

siddhi vinàyaka = Who accomplishes.

bhavabhayanàéa = Destroyer of the fear of Becoming.

suramuni vandita = Who is bowed down to by gods and sages.

**VinAYA MÀnAsAM**

**vinaya mànasam väatha pùndu taîaràn**

**vidhi vanna katha entahò! - jananì...!**

**chirakàla saêkalppam viphalamàyi pòkayò**

**mama janma vidhi pàlinì jananì...... jananì....!**

**tarumò nin pada daréanam..... (vinaya)**

```
O Mother, what may be the reason that this humble heart of
mine has been destined to languish under extreme grief? O
Mother, Dispenser of my fate, will my long standing hopes
finally prove in vain? Shall Thou not bless me with the darshan
of Thy adorable Feet?
```

**veäumoru kaâalàsu pùvupòlenne nì**

**veâiyunnò veyilèttu taîarunnu ñàn**

**azhakilla, niäamilla, maåamilla eåkilum**

**vinayattin azhivillahò! nin pàda-**

**smaraåàyi korazhi villahò! (vinaya)**

254 _Bhajanamritam 1_

```
Art Thou forsaking me as a lifeless paper flower that is
languishing under the heat of the sun? Though without beauty,
color or fragrance, this flower is ever steady in its humility and
the continued adoration of Thy Feet.
```

**charitàrtthanàkaââe! ñan nin tirusnèha-**

**parilàîa nàsvàdanattàl**

**charaåàra vindattin taåalàå enikkennum**

**éaraåam sadànandasindhò! jananì....!**

**mama janma sandàna sindhò......! (vinaya)**

```
Mother, may I be blessed with the enjoyment of the caresses
of Thy noble love. O Mother, the Ocean of Immortal Bliss, the
shelter of Thy Lotus Feet is my refuge for all times...O Mother,
Support of my life!
```

**ViÉVA ViMÒHinÌ**

**viéva vimòhinì anaévara rùpiåì**

**éàévatànandam nalkû éakti rùpinì**

```
O Enchantress of the Universe, Indestructible One, grant us the
Eternal Bliss, O Thou Whose Form is Energy.
```

**kaliyuga kalmaçama kalànàyi**

**kàraåa vastu vilaåayànàyi**

**kàminì kàñchana bhògà éakti-**

**kaîakalekkaîayù marttyà! (viéva vimòhinì)**

```
O mankind! Throwing away lust, greed and the desire for
enjoyment, be rid of the sins of the Kali Yuga and unite with
the Supreme Cause.
```

**mahatvamèäum màna vajanmam-**

**iteâuttatentinu nammaî?**

**aâutta janmam atilàtàyi**

**viéuddha vastuvilettàn**

```
Devotional songs 255
```

**taâuttiâù nì mànasa bhikçuve**

**pañcha gähangaîil ninnu (viéva vimòhinì)**

```
For what have we taken this noble human birth? In order to reach
the Pure Being and avoid another birth, prevent the wandering
mendicant of the mind from entering the house of five elements.
```

**ràvum pakalum itorupol layicha ràmakrishna**

**deva vedànta sàgara tirakaluyarttiya viéva kesariyè**

**pavitra pàvana màmà pàtayi livare nayikkyaname**

```
O Lord Ramakrishna who is immersed in That day and night,
O Light of the Universe who raised the waves of the Ocean of
Vedanta, deign to lead these people along the holy and purifying
path.
```

**pala matasàravum onnennòtiya paramasadguruvè**

**paramàrtthaêgaîeyaäiyà tuzhalunnivarkku tràåitarù**

**pavitra pàvana màmà pàtayi livare nayikkaåamè**

```
O Supreme Sadguru who told that the Essence of all religions is
the same, strengthen those who wander, not knowing the Truth.
Deign to lead them along the holy and purifying path.
```

**ViÉVAViMÒHiniYÈ**

**viévavimòhiniyè mahèévari**

**ammè namò namastè**

**éàmbhavì éòkanàéè pàdangaîil**

**nityavum kumbiâunnen**

```
Oh Enchantress of the Universe! Great Goddess, I bow to Thee.
I will bow ever at the Feet of the One who destroys the sorrows.
```

**kàîamèghatte vellum niäa**

**mèlum kàîì manòharàmgì**

**nàîìkalòcchanè nin gaîattile**

**màlayitentukondu?**

256 _Bhajanamritam 1_

```
Your black color surpasses the back color of the clouds. Your
eyes are like the flower petals. Why then do You wear that
garland around your neck?
```

**puçpangaî alla raktam**

**vamikkunna vaktrangaîallèyatu?**

**éilppikaîàru tìrttù manòhara**

**mugratayàrnna màla!**

```
Your garland is not made of flowers but of skulls oozing blood.
Which sculptor was it who made that very beautiful garland?
```

**àravamòâaâutta dàrikane**

**pàràte konnòr ammè?**

**chòrakkaîattilaâan rasamèäàn**

**kàraåam chòlliâàmò?**

```
Oh Mother, who killed the arrogant Darika, tell me Oh Mother
why do You love to dance in the pool of blood?
```

**mallare velluvànày**

**àyudham èttam karattilundu.**

**chollu chollagniyentè**

**nètrangaîilujjvali pichhiâunnu?**

```
To conquer the giants You have a weapon in Your hand. Please
tell, tell me why is there such a fire in Your eyes?
```

**àâunna pànpaåiyàn ammaykk**

**èttamàhlàdam entu kondu?**

**àbharaåangaî ètum**

**dharichiââum àrtti naéicchatillè?**

```
Why are You elated to wear a live snake around Your neck?
Was Your desire for ornaments not satiated by all Your other
ornaments?
```

```
Devotional songs 257
```

**YÀDAVAnÈ**

**yàdavanè mana mòhananè**

**àtma nàyakanè vèåugàyakanè**

**gòpì vallabhanè éyàma sundaranè**

**gòpa bàlakanè gìta nàyakanè**

**käçåa harè jaya käçåa harè**

**muraîi manòhara käçåa harè**

**käçåa harè jaya käçåa harè**

**ràdhà màdhava käçåa harè**

yàdava = One who is born in Yadu’s clan.

manamòhana = One who attracts the mind.

àtma nàyakan = Protector

vèåugàyakan = Player of the flute.

gòpivallabhan = Beloved of the Gopis

éyàmasundara = Dark complexioned beautiful One.

gòpabàlan = Cowherd boy.

gìtanayakan = Propounder of the Bhagavad Gita.

murali = Who plays the flute.

harè = Lord Vishnu

ràdhà = Sri Krishna’s Beloved.

màdhava = Goddess Lakshmi’s Consort.

**YAÉÒDA KÈ bÀlÀ**

**yaéòdà kè bàlà yadukula nàthà**

**dvàraka vàsì érì käçåà...**

**nanda nandanà navanìta chòrà**

**ràdhàvilòlà érì käçåà**

258 _Bhajanamritam 1_

**dìnà nàthà bàlagòpàlà**

**nirupama sundara érì käçåà**

**harè ràma harè ràma ràma ràma harè harè**

**harè käçåa harè käçåa**

**käçåa käçåa harè harè**

yaéòda kè bàlà = The Child of Yasoda.

yadukula nàtha = The Lord of the Yadava clan.

dvàrakavàsi = Who dwells in Dvaraka.

nandanandanà = The Son of Nanda.

navanìtachòrà = One who is fond of butter.

ràdhàvilòla = The playmate of Radha.

dìnanàthà = Lord of the downtrodden.

nirupama sundara = One whose beauty is incomparable.

```
Devotional songs 259
```

**ÉloKAs & MAntrAs**

**kàyena vàchà manas endriyair và**

**buddhyàtma nà và prakritehe svabhàvàt**

**karomi yadyad sakalam parasmai**

**nàrayanàyeti samarpayàmi**

```
I dedicate to that Supreme Lord Narayana whatever I perform
with my body, speech, mind, limbs, intellect Or my inner self
either intentionally or unintentionally.
```

**gurur brahmà gurur viçåuã**

**gurur dèvò mahèévaraã**

**guruã sàkéàt parambrahma**

**tasmai érì guravè namaã**

```
The Guru is the Lord Brahma, Vishnu and Siva. Guru is the
Supreme Absolute Itself. My obeisance to the blessed Guru!
```

**oë saha nàvavatu saha nau bhunaktu**

**saha vìryam kara vàvahai**

**tèjasvi nàva dhìtamastu**

**mà vidviçà vahai**

**òm éàntiã éàntiã éàntiã**

```
OM Lord, protect us as one, Nourish us Lord, as one. Let us
flourish in Thy strength as one. Let our knowledge, O Lord,
be changed to Light and Change our hate to love. OM Peace,
peace,peace...
```

**òë asatö mà sad gamaya**

**tamasò mà jyòtir gamaya**

**mrityòr mà amätam gamaya**

**òm éàntiã éàntiã éàntiã**

```
Lead us from untruth to Truth; From darkness to Light; From
death to Immortality.
```

260 _Bhajanamritam 1_

**òm lòkaã samastaã sukhinò bhavantù**

**òm éàntiã éàntiã éàntiã**

```
May all the beings in all the worlds be come happy. Om peace,
peace, peace.
```

**òm sarvèçàm svastir bhavatu**

**sarvèçàm éàntir bhavatu**

**sarvèçàm pùråam bhavatu**

**sarvèçàm maêgalam bhavatu**

**òm éàntiã éàntiã éàntiã**

```
May perfection prevail on all; May peace prevail on all; May
contentment prevail on all; May auspiciousness prevail on all...
```

**òë pùrnam adaã pùrnam idam**

**pùrnàt pùrnam udacyate**

**pùrnasya pùrnam àdàya**

**pùrnam èvà vasiçyatè**

**òë éàntiã éàntiã éàntiã**

```
That is the Whole, this is the Whole; From the Whole, the Whole
arises; Taking away the Whole from the Whole, The Whole
remains...
```

**òm érì gurubhyò namaã**

**hariã om**
